                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">مَنْظُورٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> A man <hi rend="ital">looked at with an evil eye:</hi> (A, TA;) <hi rend="ital">affected by what is termed a</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">نَظْرَة</foreign>; (T, TA;) i. e., <hi rend="ital">a stroke of an</hi> [<hi rend="ital">evil</hi>] <hi rend="ital">eye;</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">of an evil eye cast by a jinnee;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a touch,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">slight taint of insanity, from the jinn;</hi>] or <hi rend="ital">a swoon.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  A person, (T,) or chief person, (A,) <hi rend="ital">whose bounty is hoped for,</hi> (T, A,) <hi rend="ital">and at whom eyes glance.</hi> (A.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">مَنْظُورَةٌ</foreign> A woman <hi rend="ital">in whom is a</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">نَظْرَة</foreign>, meaning, <hi rend="ital">a fault, defect,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">imperfection.</hi> (K, * TA.)    </entryFree>26:T3fec,<entryFree id="n40038" key="نَظَرَ إِلَيْهِ" type="main">

                  </form>, (S, M, A, Msb, K,) and <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَهُ</foreign>, (M, A, Msb, K,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">نَظُرَ</orth>
                  </form>, (M, A, &amp;c.,) and <foreign lang="ar">أَنْطُورٌ</foreign> is substituted for <foreign lang="ar">أَنْظُرُ</foreign> in the dial. of certain Arabs, (IDrd, TS, K,) or, accord. to Lb, in the Bughyetel-Ámál, the <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> is here added only [by poetic license,] to make the sound of the dammeh full, agreeably with other instances; (TA;) and <foreign lang="ar">نَظِرَ إِلَيْهِ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">نَظِرَهُ</foreign>, aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">نَظَرَ</orth>
                  </form>, (A, K,) the verb being like <foreign lang="ar">سَمِعَ</foreign> accord. to the correct copies of the K, [and so in the A,] but in one copy of the K, like <foreign lang="ar">ضَرَبَ</foreign>; (TA;) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرٌ</foreign>, (S, M, A, Msb, K,) and <foreign lang="ar">نَظْرٌ</foreign> is allowable, as a contraction of the former, (Lth,) and <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَانٌ</foreign> (S, K,) and <foreign lang="ar">مَنْظَرٌ</foreign> (M, A, K) and <foreign lang="ar">مَنْظَرَةٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَنْظارٌ</foreign>, (M, K,) [which last is an intensive form; <hi rend="ital">He looked at,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">towards, in order to see, him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">he considered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">viewed, him</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it with his eye;</hi> (S, A, K;) <hi rend="ital">with the sight of the eye;</hi> (Msb;) [i. e. <hi rend="ital">looked at him</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it;</hi>] as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n40038-1" target="تنظّرهُ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n40038"/></foreign>: (K:) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n40038-2" target="انتظرهُ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> signifies the same as <foreign lang="ar">تنظّرهُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَهُ</foreign> [but app. in another sense, to be mentioned below, and not in the sense explained above, though the latter is implied in the TA; and the same may be meant when it is said that   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n40038-3" target="تنظّر" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n40038"/></foreign> is syn. with <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ</foreign>, if this assertion, which I find in the M, have been copied <pb n="2811"/> without consideration, and be not confirmed by an example]: (TA:) or <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ إِلَيْهِ</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">he extended,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">stretched,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">raised,</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">directed,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">his sight towards him</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, whether he saw him</hi> or <hi rend="ital">did not see him.</hi> (TA.) The usage of <foreign lang="ar">النَّظَرٌ</foreign> as relating to the sight is most common with the vulgar, but not with persons of distinction, who use it more in another sense, to be explained below. (TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ إِلَيْهِ نَظْرَةً حُلْوَةً</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He looked at him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">towards him, with one sweet look.</hi>] (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ فِى المِنْظَارِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He looked in the mirror</hi>]. (A.) And <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ فِى الكِتَابِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He looked into,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">inspected, the writing</hi> or <hi rend="ital">book</hi>], (A, Msb,) which is for <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ المَكْتُوبَ فِى الكِتَابِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">he looked at what was written in the writing</hi> or <hi rend="ital">book</hi>], or has a different meaning to be explained below. (Msb.) And <foreign lang="ar">هُوَ يَنْظُرُ حَوْلَهُ</foreign> [lit., <hi rend="ital">He looks around him;</hi> meaning,] <hi rend="ital">he looks much.</hi> (A.) [See also <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرٌ</foreign> below.]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَتِ الأَرْضُ</foreign>, (Sgh, K,) and <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَتِ الأَرْضُ بِعَيْنٍ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">بِعَيْنَيْنِ</foreign>, (A,) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">The earth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">land, showed</hi> (A, Sgh, K) <hi rend="ital">to the eye</hi> (Sgh, K) <hi rend="ital">its plants</hi> or <hi rend="ital">herbage.</hi> (A, Sgh, K.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ إِلَيْهِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">It looked towards,</hi> meaning <hi rend="ital">faced, him</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it.</hi> So in the Kur, [vii. 197,] <foreign lang="ar">وَتَرَاهُمْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَيْكَ وَهُمْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">لَا يُبْصِرُونَ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">Thou seest them look towards thee,</hi> i. e., <hi rend="ital">face thee, but they see not;</hi> referring to idols, accord. to A'Obeyd. (TA.) And you say, <foreign lang="ar">دَارِى يَنْظُرُ إِلَى دَارِ فُلَانٍ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">My house faces the house of such a one.</hi> (S.) And <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ إِلَيْكَ الجَبَلُ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">The mountain faced thee:</hi> (A:) as in the following ex.: <foreign lang="ar">إِذَا أَخَذْتَ فِى طَرِيقِ كَذَا فَنَظَرَ إِلَيْكَ الجَبَلُ فَخُذْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَنْ يَمِينِهِ أَوْيَسَارِهِ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">When thou takest such a road, and the mountain faces thee, then take thou the way by the right of it</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the left of it.</hi>] (S.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  [Hence, perhaps,] <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ الدَّهْرُ إِلَى بَنِى فُلَانٍ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">فَأَهْلَكَهُمْ</foreign> [app. meaning, <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">Fortune opposed the sons of such a one and destroyed them</hi>]: (S [immediately following there the ex. which immediately precedes it here:]) or <foreign lang="ar">نَظَرَ إِلَيْهِمُ الدَّهْرُ</foreign> signifies <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">Fortune destroyed them:</hi> (M, A:) but (says ISd) I am not certain of this. (M.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">النَّظَرُ</foreign> also signifies <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">The turning the mind in various directions in order to perceive</hi> a thing [mentally], and <hi rend="ital">the seeing</hi> a thing: and sometimes it means <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">the considering and investigating:</hi> [and as a subst., <hi rend="ital">speculation,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">intellectual examination:</hi>] and sometimes, <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">the knowledge that results from</hi> [<hi rend="ital">speculation</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">investigation.</hi> (El-Basáïr.) It is mostly used as relating to the intellect by persons of distinction; and as relating to the sight, most commonly by the vulgar. (TA.)
